 What will be special in every month of the year 2018 and what will be its impact on all
 aaie jaanate hai
 
 
 January - In this month the effect of Sun and Saturn will be pure
 atah naveen soch , nae vichaar or nae kaanoon jaisi tamaam chijen saamne aayengi 
 Major changes can be seen in politics
 The death of a great personality can also happen this month
 February - The effect of the cycle will be seen this month
 mahilaon ke liye maheenaa vishesh hoga 
 Large and concerted efforts to protect and improve them are expected in this month
 is maheene main jal sambandhi or jameen sambandhi aapadaaen aa sakati hanmarch- is maheene main aarthik rup se bade saare niyam ban sakate hanmhangaai main koi vishesh raahat nahin hogi 
 Big economic reforms and big scams will come out
 bahut saare nyaayik maamle is maheene sulajh sakate harrprail -surya kaa adbhut prabhaav is maheene desh main bade parivartan karvaa saktaa habade rajanetaaon ke liye is maah samasya ho sakati heis maheene rail or vayuyan durghatnaon kii sambhaavna banati hayuvaaon ke liye rojgaar ke nae avasar paidaa ho sakate hanmay -shani kaa prabhaav is maheene sabake liye raahat kii saans lekar aayega 
 People will get all kinds of relief, especially from inflation and health problems
 is maheene main yuvaaon ko rojgaar or kalyaan ke avasar milenge 
 Increase in income and prosperity of common man
 june -is maheene main logon ke vaad vivaad badhengepariwaron main tuutan or bikharaav kii ghatnaayen bad sakati hai 
 This month, nature can show a glimpse of problems like floods and earthquakes
 avivaaton ke vivaah ke liye yah maheenaa raahat de saktaa hajulai- yah maheenaa bhi kuch had tak aapadaaon or durghatnaon ke sanket de rahaa hashare bazaar main jabardast utaar chadhaav is maheene main dikh saktaa haisampatti ke kshetra main sudhaar hoga , real estate ke kshetra main sudhaar hogis maheene main dhan ke len dein ke maamle main saavdhaanee rakhni chahilgast -is maheene main mushkilen kuch kam hongelogon ke jivan main sudhaar kii sthitiyaan banengiswasthya or paariwarik maamalon main logon ko raahat milegisantan prapti or santan unnati ke liye prayaas karnaa is maheene uttam hoga 
 September- This month is showing better opportunities for career and employment
 One should work on employment opportunities in this month
 karj or aarthik sthitiyon kii samasya se logon se logon ko raahat milegiis maheene jahaan tak ho sake ghar ke bujurgon kaa dhyaan rakhana chahioctober -brihaspati ke prabhaav ke kaaran is maheene logon ke jivan main shanti aegivivaah or santan ke maamle pehle se behatar hongeis maah nyaayik sakriyata rahegi, bade mahatvapurn faisle aaengekoi bada or aitihaasik nyaayik faisla is maheene main aane kii sambhaavna banati he 
 People's expenses will increase in November-this month, little relief will also be available to people due to inflation
 Due to some changes in political form, this month may show achievements in sports world
 This last month of December-2018 will be affected by Rahu
 is maheene bina kaaran or aadhaar ke afvaahen fail sakati hai 
 There can be ups and downs for the stock market and precious metals
 Special care needs to be taken in making big decisions this month
 mujffarnagar main bhadakaau bhaashan maamle par bijepi netaa sadhvi praachi ne safai dete hue kaha he ki unhone kisi kii bhaavana nahin bhadakaai, balki maharani lakshmibai kaa kaam kiya

 i am a saint and the saint eats the bread of the society
 vahaan 'beti bachaao panchayat' thi, kisi kii bhaawanaaon ko aahat karne kaa kaarykram nahin tha
 'he said,' Just making allegations will not work
 aap mujhe video dikhaaiye
 i have pledged to protect the nation and protect the society
 maine vahaan rani lakshmibai kaa kaam kiya
 Daughters are in danger
 pashchimi uttar pradesh main tandav chal rahaa he

 in videos main upi ke sabhi bade dalon ke netaa bhadakaau baaten kehete hue camere main kaid hue hai

 kenya kii rajdhani nairobi ke westeget shopping mal main shanivaar ko hue aatankwaadi hamale main do bharatvanshiyon sahit 59 logon kii maut ho gai
 Meanwhile, on Sunday, 15 gun-toting militants of Somalia's terrorist organization al-shabaab still hold large numbers of people hostage inside the shopping mall
 is aatankwaadi hamale main 59 mauton ke alaava kareeb 175 anya ghayal hue hai
 This information was given by Kenyan Cabinet Secretary Joseph Ole Lenku on Sunday
 idhar, bharat kii rajdhani dilli main adhikariyon ne hamale main maare gaye bharatvanshiyon kii pahchaan tamilnadu ke 40 varshiya shridhar natarajan tathaa manoj jain ke aath varshiya bete paramshu jain ke rup main kii
 Foreign Ministry spokesman Syed Akbaruddin said 40-year-old Sridhar Natarajan, who hails from Tamil Nadu, and the eight-year-old son of the manager of Bank of Baroda's local branch, Paramshu Jain, were killed in the attack
 hamale main natarajan kii patni manjula shridhar bhi ghayal ho gai hai, jabaki paramshu jain kii maa mukta jain evam bahan purvi jain bhi jakhmi ho gaye hai
 Another Bharatvanshi Natarajan Ramachandran was also injured in the attack
 aadhikarik sutron ke mutabik nairobi main bhartiya ucchayukta shibabrat treepathi sahit bhartiya ucchayog ke kai varisht adhikari hamale main ghayal peediton ke upachaar kendron par upasthit the
 Indian Prime Minister Manmohan Singh on Sunday wrote a letter to Kenyan President Kenyatta condemning this heinous and disgusting terrorist attack
 kenya ke raashtrapati uhuru kenyata ko bheje ek shok sandesh main manmohan singh ne kaha, "aisi paagalpan vaali hinsa ko niyantrit karne ke liye ek thos vaishvik prayaas kii jarurat he
 " samachar agency sinhua ne kenya main sthit red cross sosayadi ke sutron ke hawaale se kaha he ki kenya ke suraksha balon evam al shabaab ke sandigdh aatankwaadiyon ke bich tanaavpurn gatirodh jari he tathaa kareeb 50 vyaktiyon kaa abhi bhi koi pataa nahin chal sakaa he
 According to President Uhuru Kenyata, some close family members have also been killed in the attack
 lenku ne kaha ki log abhi bhi imaarat ke andar maujuud hai jahaan kenya ke surakshakarmiyon ne pehali or duusari manzil ko niyantran main le liya he jabaki bandookdhaariyon ne tisare or chauthe manzil par logon ko bandhak bana rakhaa he
 The official did not specify the number of people held hostage, where mainly foreign nationals and wealthy Kenyan nationals live
 praapt khabaron ke mutabik, maare gaye videshi nagarikon main canada, france or china ke bhi naagarik shaamil hai
 Kenyan officials say 10-15 attackers have also been killed in the security operation
 raashtrapati kenyata ne shanivaar raat televijan sambodhan main kaha, "puure raashtra ke saath main mritkon ke parivaar waalon ke saath khadaa hum or sabhi deshavaasiyon kii taraf se gahari samvednaa prakat karata hum
 " ghatana kii jimmedaari lene vaale al shabaab ne twitor par likhaa, "aatankwaadi westeget mal main shanivaar dopaher ghuse or abhi bhi vahaan maujuud hai, kenyayi logon ke ghar main unke khilaaf lard rahe hai
 " iske saath hi aatankwaadi sanghathan ne hamale main 100 se adhik logon ke maare jane kaa bhi daawa kiya he
 Mikhail Margalov, chairman of the International Relations Committee of the Council of the Russian Federation, said that the Al Shabaab faction, responsible for the attack, has been operating in the East African country since February 2010 as the military wing of Al Qaeda
 sanyukt raashtra suraksha parishad or america ne bhi is aakandawadi hamale kii kadi ninda kii he
 15 members of the Security Council have spoken of standing together with the government and people of Kenya in times of crisis
 tippaniyan UN secretary-general Ban Ki-moon expressed his concern in a conversation with Kenyanatta, the President of Kenya
 britain ke videsh mantri wiliam hegg ne bhi ghatana ke prati chintaa prakat kii or ek vaktavy jari kar kaha ki vah is hamale se bhaybheet mahasoos kar rahe hai
 Apart from 59 deaths, around 175 others were injured in this terrorist attack
 yah jaankaree kenya ke mantrimandal sachiv joseph ole lenku ne ravivaar ko di
 Here, authorities in the Indian capital Delhi identified the Indians killed in the attack as 40-year-old Sridhar Natarajan from Tamil Nadu and Paramshu Jain, the eight-year-old son of Manoj Jain
 videsh mantralay ke pravaktaa saiyad akbaruddin ne bataaya ki is hamale main tamilnadu se taalluk rakhane vaale 40 varshiya shridhar natarajan or bank of baroda kii sthaneey shakha ke prabandhak ke aath varshiya bete paramshu jain kii maut ho gai he
 Natarajan's wife Manjula Sridhar has also been injured in the attack, while Paramshu Jain's mother Mukta Jain and sister East Jain have also been injured
 hamale main ek or bharatvanshi natarajan ramchandran bhi ghayal hue hai
 According to official sources, several senior officials of the Indian High Commission, including Indian High Commissioner Shibabrata Tripathi in Nairobi, were present at the treatment centers of the victims injured in the attack
 bhartiya pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne ravivaar ko kenya ke raashtrapati kenyata ko patr likhakar is jaghanya evam ghrunit aatanki hamale kii ninda kii
 In a condolence message sent to Kenyan President Uhuru Kenyata, Manmohan Singh said, "A concerted global effort is needed to control such insane violence
 " News agency Xinhua quoted Red Cross Society sources in Kenya as saying that a tense standoff between Kenya's security forces and suspected militants of Al Shabaab continued and about 50 people were yet to be traced
 raashtrapati uhuru kenyata ke mutabik, is hamale main unke parivaar ke kuch kareebi sadsy bhi maare gaye hai
 Lenku said people are still present inside the building where Kenyan security personnel have taken control of the first and second floors while gunmen have held people hostage on the third and fourth floors

 According to reports received, foreigners killed include civilians from Canada, France and China as well
 kenyayi adhikariyon kaa kahana he ki suraksha abhiyaan main 10-15 hamalavar bhi maare gaye hai
 President Kenyatta said in a Saturday night television address, "as a whole nation, i stand with the families of the dead and express my deepest condolences on behalf of all the countrymen
 " Al Shabab, who claimed responsibility for the incident, wrote on Twitter, "the terrorists entered the Westgate Mall on Saturday afternoon and are still there, fighting against them at the Kenyan home
" " Along with this, the terrorist organization has also claimed more than 100 people killed in the attack
 roosi sangh parishad kii antarrashtriya sambandh samiti ke adhyaksh mikhail marglov ne kaha ki hamale kii jimmedaari lene vaala al shabaab gut, purvi africa desh main farvari 2010 se hi alqaida kii sainya shakha ke rup main kaam kar rahaa he
 The United Nations Security Council and the United States have also strongly condemned this fanatic attack

 com / rhvguxrsd6 The enthusiasm with which humans welcomed the change in life became part of the tradition as festivals
 basant panchami rituon ke usee sukhad parivartan kaa swaagat samaaroh he
 Religiously, this festival is related to the worship of Saraswati, the goddess of learning
 sampurna bharat main bade ullas ke saath basant panchami ke din vidya kii devi saraswati kii puja kii jaati he
 The arrival of spring is considered to be the festival of Basant Panchami
 basant panchami kaa arth he shukla paksh kaa paanchvaan din
 According to the English calendar, this festival is celebrated in the month of Magh according to january-february and Hindu date
 basant ko rituon kaa raja arthath sarvshereshth ritu mana gaya he
 At this time the Panchatatva appears in a pleasant form leaving his wrath
 panchtatv maane jane vaale jal, vaayu, dharti, akaash or agni sabhi apana mohak rup dikhaate hai
 Actually, there are fascinating changes in the weather and nature that have always excited humans
 pedo par phool aa jate hai
 New coplanes emerge
 pedo main bor aane kaa sanket mil jaataa he
 These cosmic changes have always attracted poets and spring has always been the subject of poetry
 praaia: har bhashaa ke kavi ne basant kaa apni tarah se varnan kiya he
 Basant Panchami starts from Basant Panchami
 isi din shri arthath vidya kii adhishthatri devi mahasaraswati kaa janmdin manaaya jaataa he
 a fascinating story of how Saraswati saved the Devas from the demon king Kumbhakarna comes in the Uttarkand of Ramayana
 kehete hai devi se var praapt karne ke liye kumbhakarna ne das hajaar varshon tak govarn main ghor tapasya kii thi
 When Brahma agreed to give the bride, the gods said that the demons are already there, and after getting the groom, they will become even more frantic
 tab brahma ne saraswati kaa samaran kiya
 Saraswati rode on the monster's tongue
 saraswati ke prabhaav se kumbhakarna ne brahma se kaha, 'swapn varshavyanekani, dev dev mamapsinum' arthath main kai varshon tak sota rahun, yahi meri ichha he
 According to Brahmin texts, Vagdevi Saraswati is the representative of Brahma Swaroopa, Kamadhenu and all the Devas
 ye hi vidya, buddhi or gyaan kii devi hai
